<h1 class="devsite-page-title" style="width:50%" id="compose-material-3" data-text="Compose Material 3" tabindex="-1">Compose Material 3</h1>




  



  
  



  
  








<div style="align:right; text-align:right; padding-bottom:21px; margin-top:-45px; border-bottom:1px solid black;"> 
<a href="/jetpack/compose/tutorial">User Guide</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://github.com/android/compose-samples">Code Sample</a>
</div>



<div style="float:left; font-size:medium; margin-bottom:5px; margin-top:10px" class="nocontent">
<div style="text-align:left; font-size:90%; padding-right:30px; margin-right:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"> 
API Reference<br>

<a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary">androidx.compose.material3</a><br>
(<em>See the API reference docs for all compose packages</em>)

</div>
</div>

<div style="text-align:left; padding-left:10px; margin-left:10px; margin-top:15px; margin-bottom:10px;">


Build Jetpack Compose UIs with Material Design 3 Components, the next evolution of Material Design. Material 3 includes updated theming and components and Material You personalization features like dynamic color, and is designed to be cohesive with the new Android 12 visual style and system UI.

</div>



<div style="clear:both"></div>









<table style="width:100%">
<tr>
<th style="width:15%">Latest Update</th>
<th style="width:15%">Stable Release</th>

<h2 id="structure" data-text="Structure" tabindex="-1">Structure</h2>

<p>Compose is combination of seven Maven Group IDs within <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx</code>. Each Group
contains a targeted subset of functionality, each with its own set of release
notes.</p>

<p>This table explains the groups and links to each set of release notes.</p>




<table>
  <thead>
    <tr><th>Group</th><th>Description</th></tr>
  </thead>

  <tbody class="list">

    




































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-animation">compose.animation</a></td><td>Build animations in their Jetpack Compose applications to enrich the user experience.</td></tr>

  



    



























































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-compiler">compose.compiler</a></td><td>Transform @Composable functions and enable optimizations with a Kotlin compiler plugin.</td></tr>

  



    


























































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-foundation">compose.foundation</a></td><td>Write Jetpack Compose applications with ready to use building blocks and extend foundation to build your own design system pieces.</td></tr>

  



    




































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material">compose.material</a></td><td>Build Jetpack Compose UIs with ready to use Material Design Components. This is the higher level entry point of Compose, designed to provide components that match those described at www.material.io.</td></tr>

  



    



































































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material3">compose.material3</a></td><td>Build Jetpack Compose UIs with Material Design 3 Components, the next evolution of Material Design. Material 3 includes updated theming and components and Material You personalization features like dynamic color, and is designed to be cohesive with the new Android 12 visual style and system UI.</td></tr>

  



    





























































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-runtime">compose.runtime</a></td><td>Fundamental building blocks of Compose's programming model and state management, and core runtime for the Compose Compiler Plugin to target.</td></tr>

  


    



































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-ui">compose.ui</a></td><td>Fundamental components of compose UI needed to interact with the device, including layout, drawing, and input.</td></tr>

  




  </tbody>
</table>




<h2 id="declaring_dependencies" data-text="Declaring dependencies" tabindex="-1">Declaring dependencies</h2>

<p>To add a dependency on Compose, you must add the Google Maven repository to your
project. Read <a href="/studio/build/dependencies#google-maven">Google&#39;s Maven repository</a>
for more information.</p>

<p>Add the dependencies for the artifacts you need in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">build.gradle</code> file for
your app or module:</p>

<h2 id="feedback" data-text="Feedback" tabindex="-1">Feedback</h2>



<p>Your feedback helps make Jetpack better. Let us know if you discover new issues or have
ideas for improving this library. Please take a look at the
<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues?q=componentid:742043%20status:open">existing issues</a>
in this library before you create a new one. You can add your vote to an existing issue by
clicking the star button.</p>

<p><a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/new?component=742043&template=1346811"
  class="button dac-button dac-outline-button">Create a new issue</a></p>

<p>See the <a href="https://developers.google.com/issue-tracker">Issue Tracker documentation</a>
for more information.</p>
























































































































































































































<h2 id="compose_material3_common_version_10_2" data-text="Compose Material3 Common Version 1.0" tabindex="-1">Compose Material3 Common Version 1.0</h2>

<h3 id="common-1.0.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>April 17, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-common:1.0.0-alpha01</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-common-android:1.0.0-alpha01</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-common-desktop:1.0.0-alpha01</code> are released. Version 1.0.0-alpha01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943/compose/material3/material3-common">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<p>Themeless components that can be used to build Material Design components:</p>

<ul>
<li>Tonal Palette
<ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/common/package-summary#tonalpalette"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TonalPalette</code></a></li>
</ul></li>
<li>Icon
<ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/common/package-summary#icon"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icon</code></a></li>
</ul></li>
<li>Touch target size
<ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/common/package-summary#localminimuminteractivecomponentSize"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalMinimumInteractiveComponentSize</code></a></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<h2 id="compose_material3_adaptive_navigation_suite_version_10_2" data-text="Compose Material3 Adaptive Navigation Suite Version 1.0" tabindex="-1">Compose Material3 Adaptive Navigation Suite Version 1.0</h2>
<aside class="note"><strong>Note:</strong><span> As of 1.0.0-alpha07, the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite</code> package is released as part of the Compose Material3 package (Material3 versions 1.3.0-*). As a result, Compose Material3 adaptive navigation suite versioning has jumped from 1.0.0-xxxx to 1.3.0-xxxx. To find the current and future navigation suite release notes and commits, see <a href="#1.3.0">Compose Material3 Version 1.3.0</a> and later versions.</span></aside>
<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>May 1, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite:1.0.0-alpha07</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite-android:1.0.0-alpha07</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite-desktop:1.0.0-alpha07</code> are released. Version 1.0.0-alpha07 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943..fbd1ac175922f44c69a13545d194066ee428b342/compose/material3/material3-adaptive-navigation-suite">these commits</a>.</p>

<ul>

</ul>

<h3 id="adaptive-navigation-1.0.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>February 7, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite:1.0.0-alpha03</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite-android:1.0.0-alpha03</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite-desktop:1.0.0-alpha03</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6e1356c0137f362794c44812fa4f1c51dc46635f..ca2a8cf8da3a3502fccc593974f8085653e38261/compose/material3/material3-adaptive-navigation-suite">Version 1.0.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Update package name to navigationsuite from navigation-suite (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7eff77fcda4cd4d6c22361d922fb439ce7ba3a19">I7eff7</a>)</li>
<li>Material3 components exposing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> in their API have been updated to now expose a nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> that defaults to null. There are no semantic changes here: passing null means that you do not wish to hoist the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and it will be created inside the component if needed. Changing to null allows for some components to never allocate a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and allows for other components to only lazily create an instance when they need to, which improves performance across these components. If you are not using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> you pass to these components, it is recommended that you pass null instead. It is also recommended that you make similar changes in your own components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I41abb601499b4a735b6302b96cdc1f0d066dbbdc">I41abb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/298048146">b/298048146</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="adaptive-navigation-1.0.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>December 13, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite:1.0.0-alpha02</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite-android:1.0.0-alpha02</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite-desktop:1.0.0-alpha02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/03b3b94c9895b338f1b3eeec7c39f44cc72b9b89..6e1356c0137f362794c44812fa4f1c51dc46635f/compose/material3/material3-adaptive-navigation-suite">Version 1.0.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

</ul>

<h3 id="adaptive-navigation-1.0.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>November 15, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-adaptive-navigation-suite:1.0.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/03b3b94c9895b338f1b3eeec7c39f44cc72b9b89/compose/material3/material3-adaptive-navigation-suite">Version 1.0.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/adaptive/navigationsuite/package-summary#NavigationSuiteScaffold(kotlin.Function1,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,androidx.compose.material3.adaptive.navigationsuite.NavigationSuiteType,androidx.compose.material3.adaptive.navigationsuite.NavigationSuiteColors,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color,kotlin.Function0)">NavigationSuiteScaffold</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/adaptive/navigationsuite/package-summary#NavigationSuiteScaffoldLayout(kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.material3.adaptive.navigationsuite.NavigationSuiteType,kotlin.Function0)">NavigationSuiteScaffoldLayout</a></li>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/adaptive/navigationsuite/package-summary#NavigationSuite(androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,androidx.compose.material3.adaptive.navigationsuite.NavigationSuiteType,androidx.compose.material3.adaptive.navigationsuite.NavigationSuiteColors,kotlin.Function1)">NavigationSuite</a></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<h2 id="compose_material3_version_14_2" data-text="Compose Material3 Version 1.4" tabindex="-1">Compose Material3 Version 1.4</h2>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>January 15, 2025</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.4.0-alpha06</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha06 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ce211eef13c32d283bb64f2db117d93783070672..ad66672b42ec1e9359219e82b7f8189d03df40f5/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Behavior Change</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">displayCutout</code> to the group of insets that Material components take into account by default, to avoid content overlapping with the display cutout. This is a behavior change that will impact how inset-aware components behave around a display cutout. This includes the default value of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowInsets</code> parameter for inset-aware Material 3 components, and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowInsets</code> values provided in the component Defaults objects for both Material 2 and Material 3. If this change causes undesirable behavior, manually specify the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowInsets</code> parameter on a per-component basis. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I43ee9ad12db0450ebb9c65ce10d5c39d12628b6c">I43ee9</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/362508045">b/362508045</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updates to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TopAppBar</code> API. Rename the medium and large top app bars with a subtitle to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">*FlexibleTopAppBar</code>. Unified the color variations into a single <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TopAppBarDefault.topAppBarColors()</code> function, and added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">subtitle</code> color parameter to be applied for a provided subtitle Composable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I41b658469205cbb138f90fe0d35a1939c92b068f">I41b65</a>)</li>
<li>Remove <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WideNavigationRailArrangement</code> API in favor of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Arrangement.Vertical</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id034135613504c56601b4101f95633c1e3089d08">Id0341</a>)</li>
<li>Add a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalSlider @Composable</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2bfba20f1848252c3daabae8f5e944eef96af4b8">I2bfba</a>)</li>
<li>Add a new Track <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Composable</code> that allows specifying custom external track corners and track icons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I436a423b79bf88f6243fa91e02797b509996a2dc">I436a4</a>)</li>
<li>Update the floating toolbar APIs to use the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatingToolbarColors</code> object instead of a single container color. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9a054e407d8f3518c289a1a09924ce871ad0b400">I9a054</a>)</li>
<li>Add and use new experimental annotation <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExperimentalMaterial3ComponentOverrideApi</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia1eaf5578ad029fc94c5aee60146e6aebc36ca2a">Ia1eaf</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.indicatorLine</code> now takes a shape for the text field to handle clipping. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8c5f31cc77134107ae7895a273895f71ee6b2cc6">I8c5f3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/380704151">b/380704151</a>)</li>
<li>Rename the experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatingAppBar</code> functions to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatingToolbar</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1dbf88e729754da6848ed3ad571c6854812bdd57">I1dbf8</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">floatingToolbarVerticalNestedScroll</code> that can be attached to a scrollable container to update the floating toolbar expansion state based on a scroll motion that crosses a threshold. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6d65f467fb88e31233dbb9a266d8aed70d5aea32">I6d65f</a>)</li>
<li>Introducing a new API for creating a floating toolbar with an attached Floating Action Button (FAB). The API provides flexible customization options, allowing you to arrange the toolbar horizontally or vertically and place the FAB at the start or end of the toolbar. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9e3508dd059b8f6d4c5fd220d9b756ea4829d962">I9e350</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fix a Snackbar accessibility issue that caused it to announce itself on dismiss when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TalkBack</code> is on. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9db535aa1aadc875b1f9712c352e0d40c6f73fc5">/I9db53</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>External Contribution</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Commonized <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTooltip</code> in foundation and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTooltip/Tooltip</code> in material3. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifc2e61bf8dac507072ec7e52a803f40422367c68">Ifc2e6</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>December 12, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.4.0-alpha05</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha05 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6f09cf2ae979e48fdb19485f757a033e4a34bb82..604900a0795c06c6bc66e4db8d0aefb08bea3cc1/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Replace type in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WideNavigationRailState.current/target</code> value for an enum for better readability (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2d6abfd48f2111270a8006acc7c26afd8376fd11">I2d6ab</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitButton</code> change Shape api from data class to class for binary compatibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5381213967af44f2fe37dafba1f1ad0b0863a637">I53812</a>)</li>
<li>Added a tooltip API that has a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissRequest</code> parameter so makers can decide what happens when a user clicks outside of the tooltip. Deprecated the old API that doesn&#39;t contain this new parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I99aef78418a6bb25f499bd67fac956a2c87be72e">I99aef</a>)</li>
<li>Change naming of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">opticalCentering</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">horizontalCenterOptically</code>. Making the modifier internal. Replace padding parameter with max start and end offset. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0b904925a852f44df024911bb9204dc508aebdd4">I0b904</a>)</li>
<li>Change <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WideNavigationRailState</code> to have current/target value, remove enums in favor of boolean. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idfa29aad7efd1d0e943bf175f5bcb1fc347fdf0e">Idfa29</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/356039090">b/356039090</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationBarItemComponentOverride</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3a06a587c543d6a7aac7ced35adeb189c2c0deb6">I3a06a</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fix the top and bottom app-bar behaviors to reliably change color when content is scrolled all the way. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc4e834695cbd7cb8099f7b63cf21d5b764f1c81">Idc4e8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/293665988">b/293665988</a>)</li>
<li>Scroll behavior functions for top and bottom app bars now return a remembered behavior to perform better across recompositions. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0fdbe6e2ffb01d97b4c57d3a41a76f8531a2d72a">I0fdbe</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/207957336">b/207957336</a>)</li>
<li>Modifier pararemeter is now applied after internal modifiers such as dragging behavior and semantics, instead of before. This affects the ordering in which modifiers are applied. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8d83fd447173da5cd76aa6e03ca2d0b4921c7a59">I8d83f</a>)</li>
<li>Expanded bottom sheet remains expanded on size change. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2870ba38420d18b02676e6f280ef96dddc6a3a8a">I2870b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/324934884">b/324934884</a>)</li>
<li>Correctly route status and navigation bar flags for windows properties. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie674d4f080aafa8a41aeb3732797916169a07198">Ie674d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/362539765">b/362539765</a>)</li>
<li>Move modifier parameter to the scaffolds root, as documented. This aligns implementation with M2. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0235ea935c42700a5e0aa5205d0d8a7bc8ffe88e">I0235e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/372311595">b/372311595</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>External Contribution</strong></p>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>November 13, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.4.0-alpha04</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha04 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ccd90a76bd7c4acf4f4f01eca76350e383bc441e..6f09cf2ae979e48fdb19485f757a033e4a34bb82/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Revert color changes introduced in <a href="https://r.android.com/3212478">aosp/3212478</a> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">iconButtonColors</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">iconToggleButtonColors</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">outlinedIconButtonColors</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">outlinedIconToggleButtonColors</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">outlinedIconToggleButtonBorder</code>. Moved the now-reverted behavior into a new set of functions called <code translate="no" dir="ltr">iconButtonVibrantColors</code> and so forth to emphasize the high contrast colors being returned. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iffd8db14ef78fd4b4f25008be8fac97f6144bc89">Iffd8d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Introduce <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalDragHandle</code> component (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6c7701b190d72b3655c5fcad1393497936472e80">I6c770</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Rename <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissibleModalWideNavigationRailDefaults</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalWideNavigationRailDefaults</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e8775fca9c78f66e7621168e1552fc66ddc73a9">I8e877</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationBarComponentOverrides</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a3f37783f45b0c0ef72ee45439b1738eaf03e20">I8a3f3</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationRailComponentOverride</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I83e13c5643d792a173220f086cbe3899b468eb27">I83e13</a>)</li>
<li>Introduce <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WideNavigationRailState</code> to handle collapsing/expanding of the rail, allow <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalWideNavigationRail</code> to be dismissible and delete <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissibleModalWideNavigationRail</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8856843a858432a670f46a0897ffb691a4edc82a">I88568</a>)</li>
<li>Add xSmall, medium, large, and xLarge size defaults into toggle button defaults. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie95d1b6e2c56c51aa6d8d8ad66564f79e6e1acb0">Ie95d1</a>)</li>
<li>Add xSmall, medium, large, and xLarge size defaults into button defaults. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If8b6dd8a50b010dc3a3b7045a9dacea859489669">If8b6d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Filter chip trailing icon color has been updated from Primary to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OnSurfaceContainer</code>, per spec. All chip outline colors have been updated from Outline to Outline Variant, per spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I68bd4ca71c7ed6a01ee7046d3d89f617d62a4e90">I68bd4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>October 30, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.4.0-alpha03</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha03 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/955f3c40a6dc8e5772c53a0edaa2f36f94d43bb0..ccd90a76bd7c4acf4f4f01eca76350e383bc441e/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetState</code> constructor with density has been deprecated in favor of positional and velocity thresholds. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifd16e81baddd9cd4d45fbef54e69145ad52ab1c6">Ifd16e</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberTooltipPositionProvider</code> that contains an updated positioning logic. Deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberPlainTooltipPositionProvider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRichTooltipPositionProvider</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie66e2ec58567cc38fc06bb8e13ef928160db114a">Ie66e2</a>)</li>
<li>Additional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetProperties</code> allow for customization of status and navigation bar colors. By default, these update based on content color instead of system dark theme status. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib874e2b06477ef077534e5af31c1c7be97a4e134">Ib874e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/362539765">b/362539765</a>)</li>
<li>Improved the input experience for date pickers: when in input mode, the date text field will be focused for immediate text entry. The change adds a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requestFocus</code> parameter to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code>. You may prevent a focus by passing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I12d09f5f8d432ea57281466c3a6565987426404a">I12d09</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/286399710">b/286399710</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/340102743">b/340102743</a>)</li>
<li>Caching the shape defaults into the Shape object. Making the shape defaults <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Composable</code> for toggle button. Collapsing the shapes into one shape default since the variants point to the same token file. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaa0145dd90586e6f8508c4310c89bbf12f3d0313">Iaa014</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Optimize Scaffold <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentPadding</code> behavior to avoid always recomposing the body content when the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentPadding</code> changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8c8e226666d916662d5f5c22d4b02ca9ad0d6f97">I8c8e2</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/373904168">b/373904168</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldLabelScope</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">progress</code> renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">labelMinimizedProgress</code></li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldLabelPosition</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Default</code> renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Attached</code>. Interface members have been removed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If75c6603cace4c5942842b47d33544d893177672">If75c6</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> in input mode where validation errors could cause the component&#39;s height to change. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2e229559964acd9522e8a696bb0e89698c20bdd9">I2e229</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/280462363">b/280462363</a>)</li>
<li>Make the material Slider change its value when control keys are pressed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1c442dee1c87e48a2d34c0277d36a9a5d3e14a5b">I1c442</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>October 16, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.4.0-alpha02</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha02 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/fea5a8a99788fe9368f7be39aab0d1bbee389feb..b8a68b0896897fa158508d73a31998a26161d9a7/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updates to the date pickers to ensure consistent Locale usage throughout the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> when setting a Locale directly through a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerState</code> or a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePickerState</code>. Note that when setting Locales directly to the state, it&#39;s up to you to ensure that the title and headline texts are localized accordingly, as their default text will still be applied according to the default platform Locale. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I370735477b6adae8628fb967b6aa6c6138216883">I37073</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/326490763">b/326490763</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/321657276">b/321657276</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetState.isAnimationRunning</code> is now exposed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9a3d7fd89aef2731c794a8a0ee379debb6a6d77d">I9a3d7</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerColors</code> now correctly take precedence over any conflicting colors defined at the theme&#39;s Typography text styles. Also note that this update adjusts the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">color</code> parameter&#39;s position in the date picker functions and introduces a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentColor</code> parameter for customizing the header and title text colors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I30d0307b11ba2e1a02535928ab4e4131100692a8">I30d03</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/347031394">b/347031394</a>)</li>
<li>Rename <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitButton</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitButtonLayout</code> and remove <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitButton</code> color variants APIs, variants will be achieve by re-using button variants provided by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitButtonDefaults</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I44c36b66afc26ffd4a1b7d20c33b409ada12e0f8">I44c36</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> now has <code translate="no" dir="ltr">sheetGestureEnabled</code> parameter (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I856cbb6b8907ce773d47589f2c83a828a5740eb8">I856cb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/288211587">b/288211587</a>)</li>
<li>Renamed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">standardMotionScheme</code> and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expressiveMotionScheme</code> to standard and expressive. Both functions are now accessible through the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MotionScheme</code> companion object by calling <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MotionScheme.standard()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MotionScheme.expressive()</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iceccf241c8a9b729d3d7eb97432c2e2abedec332">Iceccf</a>)</li>
<li>Adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">maxWidth</code> parameter to plain and rich tooltips. It defaults to the design spec of 200 dp for plain tooltips and 320 dp for rich tooltips. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I30ce99fa9a23048859335aa781ac7b67dc92042d">I30ce9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> now correctly update the displayed month when set via their state&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">displayedMonthMillis</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If9e47133cb89ea689612133e10a31bfa20f45fd6">If9e47</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/333414302">b/333414302</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> content now moves content away from status bar. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5114c66808d155f5db97908520bad2efd93be08e">I5114c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/321877275">b/321877275</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/336962418">b/336962418</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/342093067">b/342093067</a>)</li>
<li>[Bottom Sheet] Change back callback priority to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PRIORITY_DEFAULT</code> to allow IME keyboard to dismiss first. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I447fba3df4f9178532cccf2832abd87d106f1c64">I447fb</a>)</li>
<li>Fix crashes in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> when the minimum selectable year is set to a future year. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I78656c7fcf507532603e08f4bb4ef34bdba99f87">I78656</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/319395747">b/319395747</a>)</li>
<li>Fix a date-picker issue to update the UI when an updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SelectableDates</code> instance is applied. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad59a46ee1c6484c2dc2409c9cc135070aa94bc2">Iad59a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/290135807">b/290135807</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/339898760">b/339898760</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>October 2, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.4.0-alpha01</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/fea5a8a99788fe9368f7be39aab0d1bbee389feb/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Library no longer adds a dependency to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">material-icons-core</code> so if your project relied on that, you will have to explicitly add that dependency in your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">build.gradle[.kts]</code> files. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I735ffb809330e77356492b3f63ad4bd5081cdd8e">I735ff</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/349894318">b/349894318</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationBarItem</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationRailItem</code>’s active label color change from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurface</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">secondary</code> in order to improve usability, color contrast and improve coherence within the system (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/Ibc29737146ee5534ad192db1fe7f0dfaa7a39b88">Ibc297</a>), to revert to the previous behavior, copy the default colors and change the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">selectedTextColor</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface</code>.</li>
<li>Material 3 components are now using the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MotionScheme</code> to define their motion. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie0f93b23b9623ea8f33310606359291fc6fd2b1d">Ie0f93</a>)</li>
<li>Indeterminate circular Progress Indicator motion changes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3c07e932ab6ef5bcf6fb44f136dcabd03cc830b9">I3c07e</a>)</li>
<li>Update <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedIconButtonColors</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedIconToggleButtonColors</code> for better color contrast. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I2743dfdb345ae11350bf2539f12b9f40c58ef45f">I2743d</a>)</li>
<li>Updated container and content color for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledIconToggleButtonColors</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledTonalIconToggleButtonColors</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/Ic5d0fafa3514169fd8233bd94a9bbb6b4b47deeb">Ic5d0f</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton</code> border color from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">outline</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">outlineVariant</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I1f562c325dcad2156f73a38da69619ae49057f00">057f00</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added an optional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">reverseLayout</code> parameter to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TopAppBar</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">enterAlwaysScrollBehavior</code> function to better support content that was set with a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">reverseLayout</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4e0e597d1c7f417832dd200432a64422d7775d5b">I4e0e5</a>)</li>

<li>Split button add horizontal padding for trailing button and enable optical centering calculated from start and end corner differences (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I122e287fb52270e93032d29c9ee0d3da2469ae8b">I122e2</a>)</li>
<li>Introducing a new Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MotionScheme</code> to allow setting a scheme for the component&#39;s motion. The scheme is set through the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id50c27c7dea488e88511c0e2c3ad5a67a673b038">Id50c2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Apply the correct focus traversal index to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Scaffold</code> child Composables. The order is <code translate="no" dir="ltr">topBar</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">bottomBar</code>, fab, content, snackbar. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5936be7f2f78a87a9423cff988a42c6288392603">I5936b</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue at the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> where in certain locales and format-skeletons some of the date elements (e.g. month names) did not start with a capital letter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1430f55bc95fb8e90da51057340c5004c72c4bea">I1430f</a>)</li>
<li>Integrate FAB and FAB Menu component tokens (minor visual updates to paddings and text) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib57f3f24c92774a0692758e0a46cedeebf291800">Ib57f3</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> is now first in semantic traversal order, followed by the scrim. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I436f9692595a637e75592a02304b3e2ca3a7a158">I436f9</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/358594665">b/358594665</a>)</li>
<li>Fix bottom app bar not disappearing entirely when scrolling under the navigation pill in edge to edge mode (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I3ee211d7d56465391aca50f9a694fefccb47a8e5">I3ee21</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="compose_material3_version_13_2" data-text="Compose Material3 Version 1.3" tabindex="-1">Compose Material3 Version 1.3</h2>

<h3 id="1.3.1" data-text="Version 1.3.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.1</h3>

<p>October 30, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.1</code> is released. Version 1.3.1 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/122e65c91203d7bc66192871c72c08bd149d5777..065f8f4c9800a64e5344e69e1a0aef65fa981370/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<h3 id="1.3.0" data-text="Version 1.3.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0</h3>

<p>September 4, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0</code> is released. Version 1.3.0 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/677dcf61d60ab5702e37deefb378de88774d0f8e..122e65c91203d7bc66192871c72c08bd149d5777/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.2.0</strong></p>

<p>Major features of 1.3.0</p>

<p>New Material Design 3 components</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="https://m3.material.io/components/carousel/overview">Carousel</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/carousel/package-summary#HorizontalMultiBrowseCarousel(androidx.compose.material3.carousel.CarouselState,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.foundation.gestures.TargetedFlingBehavior,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.foundation.layout.PaddingValues,kotlin.Function2)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalMultiBrowseCarousel</code></a> and <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/carousel/package-summary#HorizontalUncontainedCarousel(androidx.compose.material3.carousel.CarouselState,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.foundation.gestures.TargetedFlingBehavior,androidx.compose.foundation.layout.PaddingValues,kotlin.Function2)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalUncontainedCarousel</code></a>
Enhancements to existing Material Design 3 components.</li>
</ul></li>
<li>[<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code>] now supports Predictive Back on U+ (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iccf324cb6dfc7f4ea1fe413b69e035658282360d">Iccf32</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/281967264">b/281967264</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/304850357">b/304850357</a>)</li>
<li>[<code translate="no" dir="ltr">SearchBar</code>] now supports Predictive Back on U+ (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I657f8859433717fe5e4058bcd7a74649adece529">I657f8</a>)</li>
<li>Nav Drawer (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalDrawerSheet</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissibleDrawerSheet</code>) now supports Predictive Back on U+ as opt-in (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie5b0b1662087258f4573372df4ff600eb1a5a025">Ie5b0b</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownMenu</code> now supports custom color, shape, elevation, and border. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e9818a88b1aca1f16370c668ae60d19b0c5a89d">I8e981</a>,<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/289554448">b/289554448</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/301887035">b/301887035</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/283654243">b/283654243</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Slider to improve accessibility by adding a gap and stop indicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3058e77cfa7017a781f70e498889ab11330990af">I3058e</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ProgressIndicator</code> to improve accessibility by adding a gap and stop indicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2145171a393ef661a91799f4e1d39bdd69">I21451</a>)</li>
<li>Added a default caret for rich tooltip, support custom caret to be drawn given anchor <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutCoordinates</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifd42c2be34f72060cccce6414e28c1b2c01e025a">Ifd42c</a>)
Breaking Changes</li>
<li>New pull-to-refresh APIs:
<ul>
<li>Simplified <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshState</code> to use fractional values instead of Dp units.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">isRefreshing</code> state is controlled by the user instead of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshState</code>.</li>
<li>Separated out the nested scroll connection from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshState</code>. It is handled by the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshBox</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.pullToRefresh</code>.</li>
<li>This update is a breaking change to previous experimental APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0adeb950063988d1a05aca7aa135ccd982431423">I0adeb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/314496282">b/314496282</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/317177684">b/317177684</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/323787138">b/323787138</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/324573502">b/324573502</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/317177683">b/317177683</a>)
Visual Breaking Changes</li>
</ul></li>
<li>Update focus state overlay to be 0.1f to ensure sufficient color contrast. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7ea77012950bc900bc868cce2c2322ab86474508">I7ea77</a>)</li>
<li>Small adjustments to surface and background color defaults in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">lightColorScheme</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">darkColorScheme</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9db5226e26371223bc46f37ddfe226acf7767041">I9db52</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Slider and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ProgressIndicator</code> colors to follow the new Non-Text Contrast specs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I26807868d150434976e911f0812d3a009aa612ec">I26807</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> variants are now used by components. Components which formally calculated color with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Surface</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TonalElevation</code> now use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> roles by default, which are not affected by tonal elevation. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/304584161">b/304584161</a>)</li>
<li>Surface and Surface container baseline roles have been slightly adjusted, providing more tint in light and dark themes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I677a5570757aee5d90e3518bf379a63e3d5fba0d">I677a5</a>)</li>
<li>Promoted experimental APIs to stable!</li>
<li>Performance improvements</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.3.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-beta01</h3>

<p>May 14, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-beta01</code> is released. Version 1.3.0-beta01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/fbd1ac175922f44c69a13545d194066ee428b342..6a69101fd0edc8d02aa316df1f43e0552fd2d7c4/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DpSize</code> instead of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CaretProperties</code>. Removing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CaretProperties</code>. Rename <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CaretScope</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id9a76372b428a4114009250e322f8ee3315e3a7d">Id9a76</a>)</li>
<li>Updated the API for getting Material themed links in text. Specifically, removed the methods from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDefaults</code> for constructing themed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LinkAnnotations</code> and parse HTML with themed links. Instead, added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextLinkStyles</code> class that allows to style the links as a parameter to the Text composable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I31b93f4460f4a0a50c7a86996a499d359ba455c8">I31b93</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>May 1, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-alpha06</code> is released. Version 1.3.0-alpha06 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943..fbd1ac175922f44c69a13545d194066ee428b342/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Breaking Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>New pull-to-refresh APIs:</p>

<ul>
<li>Simplified <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshState</code> to use fractional values instead of Dp units.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">isRefreshing</code> state is controlled by the user instead of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshState</code>.</li>
<li>Separated out the nested scroll connection from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshState</code>. It is handled by the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefreshBox</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.pullToRefresh</code>.</li>
<li>This update is a breaking change to previous experimental APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0adeb950063988d1a05aca7aa135ccd982431423">I0adeb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/314496282">b/314496282</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/317177684">b/317177684</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/323787138">b/323787138</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/324573502">b/324573502</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/317177683">b/317177683</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleConfiguration#isEnabled</code> has been removed, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalRippleConfiguration</code> has been made nullable. To disable a ripple, instead of providing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleConfiguration</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isEnabled = false</code>, provide <code translate="no" dir="ltr">null</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalRippleConfiguration</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22725ce120f27f7dd0041bfabff5f3faff614ea9">I22725</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> more accurately draws scrim over status bar when edge to edge is enabled. Modal bottom sheet content can now consume window insets, allowing for visible content above the navigation bar. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> parameter <code translate="no" dir="ltr">windowInsets</code> renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentWindowInsets</code> to specify where the insets will be applied, these are no longer tied to window logic. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentWindowInsets</code> type has been changed to a function which returns <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowInsets</code>, to allow it to be resolved within its new window. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I39630f2d9a1b159ef27fa62750ffa26b00e078a0">I39630</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/274872542">b/274872542</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/300280229">b/300280229</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/290893168">b/290893168</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PrimaryScrollableTabRow</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SecondaryScrollableTabRow</code> now use custom layout instead of subcomposition, which should improve performance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I991e05b5b44b3c8bf0cd0e80c4ab5fd0d580ba46">I991e0</a>)</li>
<li>Text links got pressed state styling option in addition to normal styling, hovered and focused. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDefaults</code> methods each got a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">pressedStyle</code> argument to support that. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic473f81fd32d95ad84d6bc452c8dcbf6de7ba4ba">Ic473f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139312671">b/139312671</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Navigation drawer drag anchors now match the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">drawerContent</code>&#39;s width. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibc72f1f09657bbf2162f1ad609553dd7cc9f34ef">Ibc72f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/245355396">b/245355396</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code> top padding for label now accounts for system font size. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc78176ca566364b041b5863aa477ada660d05a9">Idc781</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed package location of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CalendarLocale</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifa235f8e3562e2cba9a0a3a90a48e76930cc9fd0">Ifa235</a>)</li>
<li>[Predictive Back] Update predictive back animations to use interpolation curve of (0.1, 0.1, 0, 1) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2591a653d70f25e4da39b39bc92bb1ac94735d31">I2591a</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>April 17, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-alpha05</code> is released. Version 1.3.0-alpha05 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/02b55f664eba38e42e362e1af3913be1df552d55..67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SearchBar</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DockedSearchBar</code> have new overloads that take a text field parameter. This allows styling the text field separately from the rest of the search bar as well as passing in custom text fields. The text field of the current implementation has been made available as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SearchBarDefaults.InputField</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I50c73509b4a67247df7240207e7ad13d5863a7ff">I50c73</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/275074248">b/275074248</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/278773336">b/278773336</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/326627700">b/326627700</a>)</li>
<li>the lambda <code translate="no" dir="ltr">drawTick</code> has been added to the public API in order to customize the ticks if needed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0c048c627d7c5a3a0dfde4b7743cdb6a2802aee9">I0c048</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Text links got pressed state styling option in addition to normal styling, hovered and focused (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5f864b3fd1b1af6ff39dee03e1aa65ede7e16d32">I5f864</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139312671">b/139312671</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CarouselItemInfo</code> to expose a mask Rect that the item is being clipped by (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I785d821b4d008bd649243c034a4df92077823667">I785d8</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTooltipState</code> from the Material 3 public API. Its functionality is combined with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipState</code> until Foundation&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTooltip</code> is stabilized. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icda29a4fd0ddd1fb4a7362464916a58ae88ef859">Icda29</a>)</li>
<li>Added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDefaults</code> object that contains methods to construct a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LinkAnnotation</code> and parse HTML-tagged string which apply <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code> to the links (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I98532f3512d1930416f66dd195746eeeba884497">I98532</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139312671">b/139312671</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenuBoxScope</code> no longer permits subclasses. Exposed dropdown menus now have a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MenuAnchorType</code> which should be passed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">menuAnchor</code> to support better a11y. This should be used instead of passing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">focusable</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenu</code>, which is now deprecated. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">menuAnchor</code> has a new parameter to control <code translate="no" dir="ltr">enabled</code> state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I55ee632daf66ef4df90297350cbff901e26ea446">I55ee6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/257209915">b/257209915</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/308840226">b/308840226</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed the border color of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton</code> when disabled. Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonDefaults.outlinedButtonBorder(&quot;enabled&quot;)</code> overload that takes the enabled state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie650bd6f38d9802f4040c0f1c90688d66446019b">Ie650b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/318461363">b/318461363</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CarouselItemInfo</code> class to help clients get information about the item sizes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9070c8284c49315b5a6d676cc235974bcf7a70c8">I9070c</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorScheme</code> constructor without surface containers is now deprecated. Please migrate to the constructor that includes surface containers. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I35c11d8e95b77a5b9c44e5103ccedc55196f65f0">I35c11</a>)</li>
<li>[Outlined]<code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldDefaults</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ContainerBox</code> renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Container</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie8d3bef9cfd4b2b8e1a355e6f167ee98e0605c16">Ie8d3b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> will no longer scroll from nested scroll if <code translate="no" dir="ltr">sheetSwipeEnabled</code> is false. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5e1c1adb83167184f2baa4457cf1b3c70272a72c">I5e1c1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/306464779">b/306464779</a>)</li>
<li>Removed some <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExperimentalMaterial3Api</code> OptIn annotation in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButtonSamples.kt</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I111d1cd1939c1788d5e216d7c09d691bd3bc9473">I111d1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>April 3, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-alpha04</code> is released. Version 1.3.0-alpha04 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a57d7d17753695012b58c9ce7ad55a8d39157e62..02b55f664eba38e42e362e1af3913be1df552d55/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Top app bar APIs now support custom heights for both fixed and collapsible sections. Fixed an issue that caused single-line top app bars to recompose too many times when scrolling content. Resolved an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MediumTopAppBar</code> truncated titles on devices with large font/display settings. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib8b0ce45ed461e7d5110e1473a90ab48c268caa6">Ib8b0c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/323403446">b/323403446</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/300953236">b/300953236</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/286296147">b/286296147</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/330410290">b/330410290</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/308540676">b/308540676</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SegmentedButton</code> and associated APIs are now stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a158168edd209070b43efc93d4ce343b9cf34fe">I8a158</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxDefaults</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxValue</code> are now marked stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7a7ac4e5e03e7e03a759ac894ad1a7e5575a9136">I7a7ac</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>March 20, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-alpha03</code> is released. Version 1.3.0-alpha03 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/638a8d3a474af45f6ad5fdc3d6d1836ea42d1778..a57d7d17753695012b58c9ce7ad55a8d39157e62/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

In particular, menus now have a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">focusable</code> parameter (default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">true</code>) that should be set to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code> when working with editable text fields. <h3 id="1.3.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>March 6, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-alpha02</code> is released. Version 1.3.0-alpha02 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e1b82c49c59d8e976ce558aba5586f6c61bc9054..638a8d3a474af45f6ad5fdc3d6d1836ea42d1778/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Making the slider states stable again. Making <code translate="no" dir="ltr">State.onValueChangeFinished</code> a val again. Wrapping <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onValueChangeFinished</code> in a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberUpdatedState</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I82ab29f469b01077eb17a70204f43b7a154abc1d">I82ab2</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/322269951">b/322269951</a>)</li>
<li>The Navigation components now use the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> roles. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawerDefaults</code> now provides distinct <code translate="no" dir="ltr">standardContainerColor</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">modalContainerColor</code> attributes. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawerDefaults.ModalDrawerElevation</code> is now <code translate="no" dir="ltr">0.dp</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7fbacfbf3b79a4077bae2b84973d6db7e1d94f2f">I7fbac</a>)</li>
<li>Removing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Stable</code> from the states of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code> since we&#39;re changing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">state.onValueChangeFinished</code> to a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">var</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ied34a92fed040ceeb5d676d6f75767ee33762cfb">Ied34a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/322269951">b/322269951</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">StandardBottomSheet</code> animation spec is now a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TweenSpec</code>, updated from a spring animation. This resolves an issue with a visible overshoot. Deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetState</code> constructors without density have now been removed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7babc194825f4cf6c05f9724eeba14d556c0840c">I7babc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/285847707">b/285847707</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> variants are now used by components. Components which formally calculated color with Surface and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TonalElevation</code> now use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> roles by default, which are not affected by tonal elevation. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/304584161">b/304584161</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed bug that caused <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ElevatedFilterChip</code>&#39;s unselected, disabled container color to be black. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I400e69a7f00c00c3c77e3fdef1e947156483731b">I400e6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/322407043">b/322407043</a>)</li>
<li>Fix indeterminate progress indicator when the progress is 0 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id658289077d4189ce18d7fc1e7cb167cc1068043">Id6582</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSlider</code> on RTL layout (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iab0e100af81859c5baaaa43ef3119113eee748ce">Iab0e1</a>)</li>
<li>Adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SliderRangeTolerance</code> for the slider range calculation since Float rounding can be inaccurate. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic918adc77cd76bd1e988e0b3e7aa92c54cf19ade">Ic918a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/324934900">b/324934900</a>)</li>
<li>Ensure that the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerDialog</code> displays its buttons when nesting a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> or when displaying any type of date picker on small screens with larger fonts. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie4758e82b94eb2d5e448a973c550302ff1601f3f">Ie4758</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/325107799">b/325107799</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277768544">b/277768544</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Menu</code> now leverages the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> role for container color. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MenuDefaults.TonalElevation</code> is now <code translate="no" dir="ltr">0.dp</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I135b7b5609dcb272a4458e14062495cca2a52ec8">I135b7</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextField</code> now leverages the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainerHighest</code> role for container color. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4dced0c76604b38aff9d58ba63f1450818054caa">I4dced</a>)</li>
<li>Elevated chips now leverage the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainerLow</code> role (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7cd2f8866db81c2c930406a631ad927b4ea755a8">I7cd2f</a>)</li>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ida75315148a0eeafda207121bd58cf5ad6ef9987">Ida753</a>)</li>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I886044e0819b603b0fc4265079bbd445759197c8">I88604</a>)</li>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I416308fdb2b68d77d41857598ce30f09ddae36fe">I41630</a>)</li>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I792c9da5cc2cee2bc06e2acd99c47162ff59e872">I792c9</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>February 21, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.3.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d9d6f951af96c8a1ab87b069a10f40b9a7b8a721..e1b82c49c59d8e976ce558aba5586f6c61bc9054/compose/material3">Version 1.3.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Update Compose M3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> to support Predictive Back on U+ (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iccf324cb6dfc7f4ea1fe413b69e035658282360d">Iccf32</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/281967264">b/281967264</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/304850357">b/304850357</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Compose M3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SearchBar</code> to support Predictive Back on U+ (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I657f8859433717fe5e4058bcd7a74649adece529">I657f8</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Slider to improve accessibility by adding a gap and stop indicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3058e77cfa7017a781f70e498889ab11330990af">I3058e</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ProgressIndicator</code> to improve accessibility by adding a gap and stop indicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2145171a393ef661a91799f4e1d39bdd69">I21451</a>)</li>
<li>Adding a default caret for rich tooltip, new rich tooltip API now allows for custom caret to be drawn given anchor <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutCoordinates</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifd42c2be34f72060cccce6414e28c1b2c01e025a">Ifd42c</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Material components have been migrated to use the new ripple APIs, and no longer query <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code>.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The fun <code translate="no" dir="ltr">drawStopIndicator</code> is now public. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3f59f30d4182bf3d296d13cf048d2077bccb35dc">I3f59f</a>)</li>
<li>Mark the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">formatWithSkeleton</code> function as internal (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic65dcccfde74a292180c92be96d69dd6468421f7">Ic65dc</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownMenu</code> now supports custom color, shape, elevation, and border. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e9818a88b1aca1f16370c668ae60d19b0c5a89d">I8e981</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/289554448">b/289554448</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/301887035">b/301887035</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/283654243">b/283654243</a>)</li>
<li>Material3 components exposing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> in their API have been updated to now expose a nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> that defaults to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">null</code>. There are no semantic changes here: passing null means that you do not wish to hoist the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and it will be created inside the component if needed. Changing to null allows for some components to never allocate a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and allows for other components to only lazily create an instance when they need to, which improves performance across these components. If you are not using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> you pass to these components, it is recommended that you pass null instead. It is also recommended that you make similar changes in your own components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I41abb601499b4a735b6302b96cdc1f0d066dbbdc">I41abb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/298048146">b/298048146</a>)</li>
<li>Adds <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleConfiguration</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalRippleConfiguration</code> to allow for per-component / sub-tree customization of ripples using fixed values. For example, to change the color of a component you don&#39;t control, or to disable a ripple for a component. In most cases the default values should be used: these APIs are an escape hatch for customization of individual components / limited sub-trees. For wider changes and custom design systems, you should instead build your own ripple using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">createRippleModifierNode</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7b5d62fd50ee78bb3559f83886aa1e7d9f964fb1">I7b5d6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/298048146">b/298048146</a>)</li>
<li>Adds new ripple API in material3 which replaces the deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple</code>. Also adds a temporary <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalUseFallbackRippleImplementation</code>, to revert material3 components to using the deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple</code> / <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code> APIs. This will be removed in the next stable release, and is only intended to be a temporary migration aid for cases where you are providing a custom <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I34cbc2834133de4f3e8dde389ed4dab8c54b0c95">I34cbc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/298048146">b/298048146</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removed subcomposition inside <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> to improve performance. Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> could crash in specific scenarios in combination with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2a198c788c55484541e5baa1a9fe2f9146e1e37c">I2a198</a>)</li>
<li>Removed subcomposition inside <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> to improve performance. Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> would crash in specific scenarios in combination with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie6401d2db363ef3377ffd16bdf456c5f0b5a1667">Ie6401</a>)</li>
<li>The badge alignment is adjusted to be closer to the center of the anchor content in respect to the top-right corner. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I18a28437cf249cd7d7ddffe103c89bdbe200399a">I18a28</a>)</li>
<li>Fix an a11y issue with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> where the Month-Year text title was conveyed as actionable to the screen reader, Switch access, and Voice access users. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2ac55010a9f9a39a8b0c3c76ed149488fba651d8">I2ac55</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">mediumTopAppBarColors</code> param order bug. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibe64a4f96541f9379e43c137c6f4f30eeaf1794a">Ibe64a</a>)</li>
</ul>

Version 1.2.1 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d9d6f951af96c8a1ab87b069a10f40b9a7b8a721..93f0ae12e7922676c5010cdc5d10f3da59640c42/compose/material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>

<li>Fix <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationBar</code> custom colors to copy from defaults. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/f660a827d39245668e4edd0a30df044d135c6733">80a779</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/326894020">b/326894020</a>)</li>
<li>Fix regression in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenu</code> to make it focusable again (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iabcf320c0fa1762463ce2fe2f38bae7ea73fcec1">3fcec1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/323694447">b/323694447</a>)</li>

</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0" data-text="Version 1.2.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0</h3>

<p>February 7, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/91bb8c1f81dcb031bda00fcd8e55f1e890b56f06..d9d6f951af96c8a1ab87b069a10f40b9a7b8a721/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

The workaround is to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRow</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRowDefaults.PrimaryIndicator</code></li>

<li>Fixed a bug introduced in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.2.0-beta02</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.cardColors</code> that did not update <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentColor</code> based on the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">containerColor</code> param value.
