<h3 id="1.2.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.2.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-beta02</h3>

<p>January 10, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-beta02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f4aac2ed38164890551d06cae49210b2afb31336..7a45f0bc9e0a73744b3780a6f92e1b570de58bba/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Known Bug</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>A bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButtonColors</code> will by default assign <code translate="no" dir="ltr">disabledContentColor</code> to an alpha (0.38f) of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalContentColor</code> instead of the user specified <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentColor</code>. The workaround is to explicitly set the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">disabledContentColor</code>. This will be fixed in the next release.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Adding the capability to enable tooltip carets for Plain <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Tooltip</code> APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibf767f249315a4c4c327b62a487c6770435c13c7">Ibf767</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberSwipeToDismiss</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue</code> are all renamed to have <code translate="no" dir="ltr">_SwipeToDismissBox_</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I68d6dcb43013ec07c340276c0f578960a80bd0d1">I68d6d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListItem</code> end padding value to align with spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibd68bcdc69da576e47b83fa793c0d626874aa4be">Ibd68b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/305342674">b/305342674</a>)</li>
<li>Outline color for outlined card is now correctly mapped to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlineVariant</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I754802e26a95258d2c3b5b0d9e3030f64b9b630f">I75480</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/310979715">b/310979715</a>)</li>
<li>Dynamic color now pulls from system defined color roles. This improves contrast for accessible content, and more closely aligns dynamic color to the Material spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1de966bfc4f27259e1f07244ad10bc4c01b520f3">I1de96</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> back handling on Android T/13+ when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">android:enableOnBackInvokedCallback=&quot;true&quot;</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I728dc69c651c3b9d44857037ff8047ee67f13430">I728dc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/306196110">b/306196110</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.2.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-beta01</h3>

<p>December 13, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/064f85294a9be2e86650737b91db1bff868926e2..f4aac2ed38164890551d06cae49210b2afb31336/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Mark <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabIndicatorScope</code> as experimental. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I45c88927d22d78743fe50f332addc9433454292a">I45c88</a>)</li>
<li>Removing deprecated experimental APIs for tooltip. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I438cbd0987e03da47d55eca56c8617c0c7b6f941">I438cb</a>)</li>
<li>Change new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRow</code> overloads to not use subcompositions. This results in a different way to build the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRow</code> indicators with custom modifiers provided. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ife741ac95e65785e0f0673ab65414b7f74971d6d">Ife741</a>)</li>
<li>Deprecate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissDirection</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissValue</code> API&#39;s. These have been merged to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue</code>, whose values indicate both position and direction of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissState.progress</code> is now marked as a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatRange</code> between <code translate="no" dir="ltr">0.0</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.0</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissState</code> deprecated Saver and Constructor have now been removed. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code> component, state and defaults object have been remarked as experimental. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib54f2c6707fdf2fa10fb5c19166c583f24c2bc6f">Ib54f2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The default indicator for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullToRefresh</code> is now an open arrowhead instead of a solid triangle. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I67be3e670a96c3aa42d9c760fe318739dfb45650">I67be3</a>)</li>
</ul>

<li>Adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetProperties</code>. Moving <code translate="no" dir="ltr">securePolicy</code> into <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetProperties</code>. Adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isFocusable</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">shouldDismissOnBackPress</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetProperties</code>. These new booleans help determine how modal bottom sheet should handle IME events. <h3 id="1.2.0-alpha09" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha09" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha09</h3>

<p>October 4, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha09</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/91bb8c1f81dcb031bda00fcd8e55f1e890b56f06..80156d02f56222d46dbad403c3adb812faaf62d6/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha09 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Migrated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalNavigationDrawer</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissibleNavigationDrawer</code> to use new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnchoredDraggable</code> APIs. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawerState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> has been replaced by the open and close methods, and the offset is now exposed as a float instead of a state object. You can access the offset directly through <code translate="no" dir="ltr">currentOffset</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0a72c377bd15770825efdce43c63a84ddfbeb0f4">I0a72c</a>)</li>
<li>Non-Composable functions have been added for creating a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePickerState</code> directly. These functions can be used as an alternative to the Composable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberDatePickerState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberDateRangePickerState</code> functions when needed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I703262a5a9d3e87da82adf1c9993b462cd8d941a">I70326</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/291524052">b/291524052</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed and Scrollable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRows</code> now have Primary and Secondary variants. These correctly map to the color and indicator behavior as defined in Material3.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PrimaryScrollableTabRow</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SecondaryScrollableTabRow</code> now expose scroll state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iec8f5a2876a15865842a6f0d4a584b539e16892a">Iec8f5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/260572337">b/260572337</a>)</li>
<li>Adding a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">sheetMaxWidth</code> parameter that developers can set to specify a maximum width that the sheet will span. Dp.Unspecified can be passed in for the parameter if a sheet that spans the entire screen width is desired. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifb7c9ee4d0066e86787e8fcbf0d156b9f92e5cfb">Ifb7c9</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266697696">b/266697696</a>)</li>
<li>Adding back <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltipBox</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RichTooltipBox</code> APIs as deprecated methods. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I246fa14bd02246c864f1db1b98e34a352fd32e55">I246fa</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fix a crash when the<code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> is initialized with a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerFormatter</code> that has certain date skeletons that stay the same when converted to date patterns (such as YY). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I01f2902849d4dd5c2426f4d3c13f52463692e3f4">I01f29</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>September 20, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha08</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9ce75ea1baa2af10dda8f787f69c40c6654bcac1..91bb8c1f81dcb031bda00fcd8e55f1e890b56f06/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Behavior Breaking Change</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorScheme</code> is now Immutable, making individual color updates less efficient, but making more common usage of colors more efficient. The reasoning behind this change is that the majority of apps wouldn&#39;t have updating individual colors as a main use case.
This is still possible but it will recompose more than before, in turn we significantly decrease the amount of state subscriptions through all of Material code and will impact initialization and runtime cost of more standard use cases. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic447d95734c3399733c49f4b6d018ec296fc251a">Ic447d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/297212873">b/297212873</a>)</li>
<li>Tonal Elevation no longer animates in different interaction states to match spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icdd12f4e11256ea166b3f4808f05228c28442ae7">Icdd12</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomAppBar</code> that takes as parameter a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomAppBarScrollBehavior</code> in order to auto-hide it when content is scrolled. Also added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FabPosition.EndOverlay</code> allowing the FAB to overlay the bottom app bar in the scaffold instead of being anchored above it. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iecb47accb59cbf44a49d0099289ef89736a84f2b">Iecb47</a>)</li>
<li>Added a simple Label component that builds on top of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTooltipBox</code> that won&#39;t dismiss when tapping outside of the bounds of the label. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I821f9f124e3d1933f3fc629c106d48d157929079">I821f9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removed the use of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberSaveable</code> for tooltips. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icc131c852cc3b3c722954aecb0a002711e13ca96">Icc131</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/299500338">b/299500338</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced a temporary flag to control whether Scaffold should measure its children during measurement or during placement. By default, this will measure in measurement. If you are facing issues with the new behavior, please file an issue. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0b354a595fa56d96c4d48cfae5b394c7203bd23c">I0b354</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed horizontal Edge to Edge in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheet</code> by using the correct measurement for device screen width. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1df0cdf2ec735c17b914aee04ed20d54a1896573">I1df0c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/299058752">b/299058752</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> was not calling <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissedRequest</code> when dismissing it by swiping down on the sheet. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idfdd8b490caed6486292ae244ba9e4e9fb813f96">Idfdd8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>September 6, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha07</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3315f1ef094c312203fe26841287902916fbedf5..9ce75ea1baa2af10dda8f787f69c40c6654bcac1/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Auto-mirror icons support has been added in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">compose material 1.6.0-alpha05</code>, please see the  <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material#1.6.0-alpha05">release notes</a> for details on auto-mirror icons.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SliderState</code> implements <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DraggableState</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9b11656ba75c1f01060265735a75280858d5f4ae">I9b116</a>)</li>
<li>Change shape to be a required param. Rename <code translate="no" dir="ltr">position</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">index</code> in shape helper function. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3494194f783157e24a10b643083fb99ff41777b9">I34941</a>)</li>
<li>Updates the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">formatWithSkeleton</code> to include a map that is used as a cache for performance improvements. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3195fdb04c8cab7fdf9bcf6e5cfd03d9a5700343">I3195f</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTooltipBox</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">compose.foundation</code> and updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltipBox</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RichTooltipBox</code> to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipBox</code> with new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RichTooltip</code> composables. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I79e1df0ac02fdccc3399dcf8d24a515d6461fde9">I79e1d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">dynamicLightColorScheme</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dynamicDarkColorScheme</code> now return higher chroma colors for surface and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">surfaceContainer</code> roles. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5e90155620f5f6a5adbe5df4288a249744ba1699">I5e901</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where some components using Subcomposition (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>) inside a Scaffold inside a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code> were attempting to read their size too early. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I297b401ce6fd3b01ac5a2fba5fd617f66bc34550">I297b4</a>, <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I871f1f655d0bf504490a040ec793b1b07ce195e4">I871f1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/295536718">b/295536718</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>August 9, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313..5d7dd999525725bd038a00ca4e89e0fef624a6da/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CheckboxDefaults.colors()</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">disabledUncheckedColor</code> now only affects the border of the checkbox. Special cases that require you to set the internal box color when disabled and unchecked requires a custom constructed instance of a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CheckboxColors</code> with the desired color values. <h3 id="1.2.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>July 26, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494..4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Experimental Segmented Button API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifc8fb7a7aba0f8712ed6f0b8508cb21f803795bb">Ifc8fb</a>)</li>
<li>Dividers now have a parameter to control orientation to support vertical dividers. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4c8999504b8f853c5c898fd960d5b4a0e9c02491">I4c899</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/288438593">b/288438593</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We are moving the density dependency to the component level. This applies to the following components: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code> and Sheet based components. Please use the new overload provided where density is a parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1846ea6aeb659f53eb8bff6895f7aea19af46fe8">I1846e</a>)</li>
<li>Additional annotations to specify allowed inputs to composables (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ief2342371876dcbdeed01122dd533759d189a01e">Ief234</a>)</li>
<li>Add an icon parameter to segmented button, split semantics so that segmented buttons can be selectable to implement single-select, and toggleable to implement multi-select, with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SelectableSegmentedButtonRow</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggelableSegmentedButtonRow</code> respectively. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38740a995876133539f108629cf9a82d02c49cc2">I38740</a>)</li>
<li>Divider has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalDivider</code>. Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalDivider</code> functionality. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5975c8c0a45299f1b2ad5f9be6f77f4f1f04542b">I5975c</a>)</li>
<li>Change the use of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ClosedFloatingPointRange</code> for the lighter weight <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatRange</code> in experimental Material3 APIs to minimize autoboxing. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4aab509d1a5302f50556bd187882587eacc985b5">I4aab5</a>)</li>
<li>Added new Start alignment for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FabPosition</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib7aea97d6ac5c6ee33fd10916c74c540ff5889de">Ib7aea</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/170592777">b/170592777</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> respects local layout direction. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib4f44471ba73a6fbbbdb28e73ea876b91618c406">Ib4f44</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/285628622">b/285628622</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>June 21, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/c5bf9bc40dd5d9f0b3f34e7273ac0d4e4f05c41d..3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> is now <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code> by default in Material 3 typography. The default line height style has also been changed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Trim.None</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Alignment.Center</code>, and explicit <code translate="no" dir="ltr">lineHeight</code> (in sp) have been added to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code>s of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Typography</code>. Consult <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/compose/text/style-paragraph#adjust-line-height">the API docs</a> if you want to customize these values, and see <a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/fixing-font-padding-in-compose-text-768cd232425b">the blog post</a> for an in-depth explainer of these changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6266fefa603c4079ec506a53d1372cebcc8dc50e">I6266f</a>, <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icabc31f64e23ba0b8b92c909a8df1fe5f72ce9ed">Icabc3</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added an overload for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSlider</code> that is a stateful version of the component. Created <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSliderState</code> that holds all of the information for the current active track, the measurements of the components of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSlider</code>, and the drag and gesture logic. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8c270fd01856f713bb5a40bf356f2875e64fd6e1">I8c270</a>)</li>
<li>Search bar now supports shadows via the newly added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">shadowElevation</code> parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia5369b93f692ff1289148eb13a0fd0c44af8ec4e">Ia5369</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/271040353">b/271040353</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorScheme</code> now supports new <a href="https://material.io/blog/tone-based-surface-color-m3"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SurfaceContainer</code> roles</a>.</li>
<li>Surface tonal elevation overlay can now be disabled with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTonalElevationEnabled</code> composition local. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic203c029337ab0892d1efdbecef069ad3c771f46">Ic203c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277774590">b/277774590</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Open the component colors constructors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8c4a6ce56fb4a77a1e3eb17c6cad139b16bdc6ff">I8c4a6</a>)</li>
<li>Adding focusable parameter to both tooltip APIs, so that developers can have the tooltip consume touch events or not. Be cautious that this might break accessibility focus automatic traversal. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie32d8060e23253e7e7763ac882b07c8f54b113a3">Ie32d8</a>)</li>
<li>Optimized accessibility for performance and memory allocations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iede48198c2709b0736a39287ebc8f082d3869ae2">Iede48</a>)</li>
<li>Expose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultSizeClasses</code> and create <code translate="no" dir="ltr">StandardSizeClasses</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowSizeClasses</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9183896b65cae68d142f0d4c2e8a023a958eb082">I91838</a>)</li>
<li>change <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowWidth/HeightSizeClass</code> to float value classes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie686e093b760eb4e7bc055b03b848b026221554a">Ie686e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Scaffold&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentWindowInsets</code> parameter now respects consumed window insets. Note that the behavior of content padding based on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">topBar</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">bottomBar</code> remains unchanged when these parameters are provided. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I08b739c22d2f2ac541801ae92e466ae41f265ff4">I08b73</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/264601542">b/264601542</a>)</li>
<li>Fix the alignment of the center top app bar to ensure that a long title doesn&#39;t render over the action icons or the navigation icon. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4369f6c51c711129bb30b1de58684131b02499ae">I4369f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/236994621">b/236994621</a>)</li>
<li>Tab positions now enforce a minimum content width of 24.dp. This provides an accessible touch target for tab indicators. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id8861dce93609e920311f95b31151a778cc06222">Id8861</a>)</li>
<li>Dynamic color palettes from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dynamicLightColorScheme</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dynamicDarkColorScheme</code> now support new surface roles. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1252ebaf56aa26fab7a211ffcb0df306ab831b4d">I1252e</a>)</li>
<li>Updating the badge notification alignment to not clip when colliding with great grandparent. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idf75aadf4f6e06f3697ca2ae8420681772f7b48e">Idf75a</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>May 24, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-*:1.2.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/258b72327bc8e1d5a2205e37886d37e4de48495a..c5bf9bc40dd5d9f0b3f34e7273ac0d4e4f05c41d/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add window insets parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code>.
<ul>
<li>Scrim for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> may now be drawn behind status bar with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">windowInsets</code> set to zero</li>
<li>Updated default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> functionality to stay outside of system bars including navigation</li>
<li>Status bar inset handling is provided by drag handle in edge-to-edge mode.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetDefaults</code> includes window insets for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetWindow</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I312008e48573ebd21326f77216be0bcd0372aa78">I31200</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/274872542">b/274872542</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272973615">b/272973615</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272334475">b/272334475</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268432129">b/268432129</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/275849044">b/275849044</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/275486106">b/275486106</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268433162">b/268433162</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
<li>Deprecate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Indicator</code> and add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Primary</code>/<code translate="no" dir="ltr">SecondaryIndicator</code> to match the M3 specs. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PrimaryIndicator</code> matches the width of the tab&#39;s content whereas <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SecondaryIndicator</code> spans the full available width. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SecondaryIndicator</code> is equivalent to the now deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Indicator</code> and can be a direct replacement. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I27604bde8305f90ea2549993df676c92babfbaef">I27604</a>)</li>
<li>Added an option to pass in a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollState</code> when constructing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownMenu</code> or an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenu</code> for controlling the vertical scroll state of the displayed menu items. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia0734c832441988ff0047f25719d7c8edae8db5c">Ia0734</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/185304441">b/185304441</a>)</li>
<li>Added an overload for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code> that is a stateful version of the component. Created <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SliderState</code> that holds all of the information for the current active track, the measurements of the components of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code>, and the drag and gesture logic. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I124a5957177062146d7994a115c486a299f1bbb3">I124a5</a>)</li>
<li>Renaming the Semantics property <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isContainer</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isTraversalGroup</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I121f64d7e7be332c41a1fbf10a70ef1ec14ce0dc">I121f6</a>)</li>
<li>Added optimized <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle.merge(...)</code> with full parameter list. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad23419809af1c7405ba9a9d42569521e7647034">Iad234</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/246961787">b/246961787</a>)</li>
<li>Made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RichTooltipState</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltipState</code> public interfaces. Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RichTooltipStateImpl</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltipStateImpl</code> for default states. Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">remember*State</code> functions to obtain these implemented states. Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipSync</code> in favor of an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipDefault.GlobalMutatorMutex</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7813de158d25c43169dfb12cdf6b183332f753d9">I7813d</a>)</li>
<li>Updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerColors</code> to include additional customization options for the date picker divider, navigation, and text input fields colors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1a6856afd9a84e2aec18ece4ed6646b7f4ff4079">I1a685</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/274626815">b/274626815</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerState</code> and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePickerState</code> are now public interfaces with default implementations that can be retrieved by the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberDatePickerState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberDateRangePickerState</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I71c523826e8295772291dd5e3459c50037ac14a7">I71c52</a>)</li>
<li>Removed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dateValidator</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> and introduced a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SelectableDates</code> interface that can be set on the state to control which dates or years are selectable in the UI. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic2fc6f681417f632e7279016bd67ccbe372d653e">Ic2fc6</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePicker</code> removed from stable API, further changes are expected in the state API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3f39a13a8cfd4ae5fdc2c05b644452b7bceea963">I3f39a</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> moved to android only. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> is not recommended for desktop use, and the functionality is not actively maintained. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib37784ddf10366ce34ecbcab3bcf15cc534b26fc">Ib3778</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> dismiss action to appear below the confirm action when the actions stacked over each other to fit into the dialog&#39;s width. This fix aligns the implementation with the Material Design spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I029ded5c6dd79f38b1a060afb3d24dcfb9cf119a">I029de</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235454277">b/235454277</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListItem</code> using incorrect padding for three-line items. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6e235866f4f873b16a0d5f8e37fdc7f4370b76aa">I6e235</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> now can display IME keyboard (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc5082008acb547cac2100a69cab4be7db85f50f">Idc508</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/262140644">b/262140644</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268380384">b/268380384</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272483584">b/272483584</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>May 10, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.2.0-alpha01</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.2.0-alpha01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a2cccd4facfdd7aba23b74cfb5253196d1c0fc31..6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68/compose/material3">Version 1.2.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h2 id="version_11_2" data-text="Version 1.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1</h2>

<h3 id="1.1.2" data-text="Version 1.1.2" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.2</h3>

<p>September 20, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.2</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.2</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/28298029d8a95189089eace9273d608da3c6b81a..444f88fb647c26b3426a9a95eac755624463514e/compose/material3">Version 1.1.2 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed modifier incorrectly being passed to two composables. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issue?id=282761472">b/282761472</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePickerState</code> returns incorrect hours when initialized with 23 hours. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issue?id=278242122">b/278242122</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed initial toggle state for noon and minute validation. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issue?id=269768197">b/269768197</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issue?id=282790635">b/282790635</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">state.hour</code> returning incorrect value for 11pm. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issue?id=282761472">b/282761472</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issue?id=278242122">b/278242122</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.1" data-text="Version 1.1.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.1</h3>

<p>June 21, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.1</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.1</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/27c69a0a8f6f433a0e969ff934e622adcfd5a947..28298029d8a95189089eace9273d608da3c6b81a/compose/material3">Version 1.1.1 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Adds call for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> without <code translate="no" dir="ltr">windowInset</code> param for binary compatibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib79592db8c08b657aae3b46c51f708a57d7e52d6">Ib7959</a>)</li>
<li>Add window insets parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code>.
<ul>
<li>Scrim for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> may now be drawn behind status bar with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">windowInsets</code> set to zero</li>
<li>Updated default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> functionality to stay outside of system bars including navigation</li>
<li>Status bar inset handling is provided by drag handle in edge-to-edge mode.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetDefaults</code> includes window insets for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetWindow</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I312008e48573ebd21326f77216be0bcd0372aa78">I31200</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/274872542">b/274872542</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272973615">b/272973615</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272334475">b/272334475</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268432129">b/268432129</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/275849044">b/275849044</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/275486106">b/275486106</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268433162">b/268433162</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0" data-text="Version 1.1.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0</h3>

<p>May 10, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a2cccd4facfdd7aba23b74cfb5253196d1c0fc31..27c69a0a8f6f433a0e969ff934e622adcfd5a947/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Major features of 1.1.0</strong></p>

<p><strong>New Material Design 3 components</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><a href="https://m3.material.io/components/bottom-sheets/overview">Bottom sheets</a>
<ul>

</ul></li>
<li><a href="https://m3.material.io/components/date-pickers/overview">Date pickers</a>

<li><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#DatePicker(androidx.compose.material3.DatePickerState,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,androidx.compose.material3.DatePickerFormatter,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function0,kotlin.Function0,kotlin.Boolean,androidx.compose.material3.DatePickerColors)">DatePicker</a>, <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#DateRangePicker(androidx.compose.material3.DateRangePickerState,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,androidx.compose.material3.DatePickerFormatter,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function0,kotlin.Function0,kotlin.Boolean,androidx.compose.material3.DatePickerColors)">DateRangePicker</a>, <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#DatePickerDialog(kotlin.Function0,kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Shape,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp,androidx.compose.material3.DatePickerColors,androidx.compose.ui.window.DialogProperties,kotlin.Function1)">DatePickerDialog</a></li>

<ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-rc01</h3>

<p>April 19, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-rc01</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-rc01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/258b72327bc8e1d5a2205e37886d37e4de48495a..a2cccd4facfdd7aba23b74cfb5253196d1c0fc31/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePicker</code> removed from stable API, further changes are expected in the state API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3f39a13a8cfd4ae5fdc2c05b644452b7bceea963">I3f39a</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> moved to android only. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> is not recommended for desktop use, and the functionality is not actively maintained. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib37784ddf10366ce34ecbcab3bcf15cc534b26fc">Ib3778</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.1.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-beta02</h3>

<p>April 5, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-beta02</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-beta02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553..a200cb82769634cecdb118ec4f0bfdf0b086e597/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetState</code> now has optional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">skipHiddenState</code> parameter</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberStandardBottomSheetState</code> now has optional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">skipHiddenState</code> parameter</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> now has a defined Hidden anchor, though it is disabled by default</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetState.requireOffset</code> documentation has been updated</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetDefaults.MinimizedShape</code> has been renamed as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetDefaults.HiddenShape</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I839f464c556eafb1b6fd823134da46943475919d">I839f4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/273870234">b/273870234</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Do not switch the dial face from hour to minute when touch exploration is enabled. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I717d015a566423b1006a9549dbc6850cde3ae356">I717d0</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> drag handle semantics are now merged. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I05afb36b9bd2f2cff6127478b1be715450aff687">I05afb</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> modifier, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">containerColor</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentColor</code> parameters now only affect content. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I992cb8a410e827be2e97f35e64f3070320abc1cb">I992cb</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold nestedScroll</code> for sheet content now implements flings. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I992cb8a410e827be2e97f35e64f3070320abc1cb">I992cb</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-beta01</h3>

<p>March 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-beta01</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-beta01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ba23752ee1dc6eae18f1350f0815ed79d605e9c5..5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add layout type param to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePicker</code> composable. It allows to use different layouts, depending on the screen configuration (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia0e164e18f9be63fd93446f03e0eb24f435ed4d2">Ia0e16</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SearchBarDefaults</code> has been marked as experimental. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I65561ee442e307fed389d8379982354af729acab">I65561</a>)</li>
<li>Added shadow elevation to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I94e0f2e736f142ce44b97ca1f86ad70640efd9d3">I94e0f</a>)</li>
<li>Added support for displaying the date pickers without the header part. API changes to allow passing a null headline when creating a date picker. You can now pass null headline, title, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showToggleMode = false</code> in order to display a headless picker. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id3f3a800c84c12f7c96a3654e59258933da0ec0b">Id3f3a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266132421">b/266132421</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/267194809">b/267194809</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Search bars now automatically clear focus when made inactive. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22a7c93c7d06f39b6413c3f1d40f141b0d141fd8">I22a7c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261444487">b/261444487</a>)</li>
<li>Updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> to allow selecting a range with the same date for its start and end. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I16529402422cca8b5a370483fa14e4f429548e7c">I16529</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272882497">b/272882497</a>)</li>
<li>Text fields now properly position their text elements when font size is smaller than expected. This may result in a few pixels change in your apps based on font settings and script. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8b8d0c81e2882446a0fb3e68e1744efc07cb990d">I8b8d0</a>)</li>
<li>Bottom sheet semantic actions now have labels. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I277b088568cf9f3a3448386d5da1b32425b83c05">I277b0</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>March 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha08</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha08</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522..ba23752ee1dc6eae18f1350f0815ed79d605e9c5/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffoldState</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I063d432e10628475a8c902cd30e75f12fd40d99c">I063d4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added functionality to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePickerState</code> and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePickerState</code> to allow setting dates after the initial creation of the state, as well as resetting selections by setting null timestamps. Setting dates manually should be made with caution, and the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">setSelection</code> function will throw an exception in case a provided date fails a precondition (see documentation). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifa6451a9e32ad031ac3223cb8b5fea132a2d0191">Ifa645</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268609314">b/268609314</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/270427389">b/270427389</a>)</li>
<li>Rename Collapsed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetValue</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PartiallyExpanded</code> to more accurately and flexibly depict behavior in this state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia1491d68dc636ca9d80a31372a64e63f69ee4013">Ia1491</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListItem</code> parameter names to _content instead of _text. Default getters are now <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ReadOnlyComposables</code> where relevant. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I69a252e0a5bc6ebb63c7be08746ace65dfe02d62">I69a25</a>)</li>
<li>Graduate interactive Surface APIs from experimental. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I90d596d5aa4141884f1b7878ae61053aa4fc7161">I90d59</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261561812">b/261561812</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HalfExpanded</code> state was calculated incorrectly and the sheet would appear to be floating. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I45e84ba00263f4bea61a3abac54bf05a6494bce8">I45e84</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268411386">b/268411386</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmValueChange</code> check to scrim tap for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2311a043ffbac63c4278fce9d0e73450fc808201">I2311a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/270425759">b/270425759</a>)</li>
<li>Move semantic <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheet</code> actions to drag handle. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I158bae5303952975da627224926043322175c1a2">I158ba</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> now commands focus on launch, handles back button. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4d2ab70ac620fd98835125b84794ce24dfcf5ebd">I4d2ab</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet onDismissRequest</code> is now also handled during nested scroll flings. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I655c581c067056b1815fe50befd32333c78e30bb">I655c5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/268433166">b/268433166</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>February 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha07</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha07</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677..87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add a Time Input composable that works with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberTimePickerState()</code>, it follows the M3 spec for time input (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia4fab49a74980251b5dee8d9dacacf2012811c7d">Ia4fab</a>)</li>
<li>Added a Material 3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> API for selecting a range of dates. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7a6c3bd20c0330eec911786619dcc7b86c3dad04">I7a6c3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/267194809">b/267194809</a>)</li>
<li>Added a Material 3 input mode support for selecting date ranges via the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code> API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifdbc4d78f6e5029ae68c6d30d80a843f30843309">Ifdbc4</a>)</li>
<li>Text field colors now allow customizing:
<ul>
<li>The input field and placeholder text colors based on focus and error state. The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">textColor</code> parameter has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">unfocusedTextColor</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">placeholderColor</code> has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">unfocusedPlaceholderColor</code>.</li>
<li>The container color for filled text fields based on error state with the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">errorContainerColor</code> param.</li>
</ul></li>
<li>Exposed dropdown menu text field colors have been updated with parameters to support the new prefix and suffix API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9c8b4f070921d64f8a7a3ac74074c12d7773348b">I9c8b4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254284181">b/254284181</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/264766350">b/264766350</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Reverting some Slider API versions and removing redundant Slider overloads that are covered by the new experimental Slider with custom thumb and track. Promoting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSlider</code> to be stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie8fbdf564fa3e2a83ff891a79bc0baa5c12e586d">Ie8fbd</a>)</li>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">defaultElevation</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">elevation</code> in chip&#39;s elevation functions. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0f87254cdb91bec8c6ace6fd3883342733755ad9">I0f872</a>)</li>
<li>The following Material 3 text field APIs are no longer experimental: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextField</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">textFieldWithLabelPadding</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">textFieldWithoutLabelPadding</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">outlinedTextFieldPadding</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieb5c0ab1f3270ee3fd45265f143f49a5cdaa2d08">Ieb5c0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261561819">b/261561819</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePickers</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">is24Hour</code> uses system setting (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I18856a395db9ce7e4dbd099299ded52407fd2873">I18856</a>)</li>
<li>Removed experimental annotation from scaffold apis. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibb51eaf53f07ec6407de4acd4a3174137b171d1e">Ibb51e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261565765">b/261565765</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261436953">b/261436953</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> default shape is now always <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetDefaults.ExpandedShape</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0dfcaa455e676e5280abb399db53e31a61870679">I0dfca</a>)</li>
<li>Accessibility improvements for Material 3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> and  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DateRangePicker</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5087ec38bd740387f9b42197f72511d0eda4b0c7">I5087e</a>)</li>
<li>Fix bug where max height constraint is propagated and may crash. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I30d8c5eb63c4c9a5078cb10e5a591d6ac2c8a065">I30d8c</a>)</li>
<li>Removed semantic roles from clickable and selectable surfaces, updated components that used them to set roles using modifier.semantics (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I793d92a6d882bb8d0cae537a365709f9483e950d">I793d9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>February 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha06</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha06</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e5dad1e7d1c225f89f7c2d5a39a7a0de8d637d7b..f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Text fields now support prefix and suffix text (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia85786c582981e8f16a7053a869e06c2c1a43fb8">Ia8578</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179884561">b/179884561</a>)</li>
<li>Added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePicker</code> function to show a time picker following the Material 3 spec, used in conjunction with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePickerState</code> and convenience method <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberTimePickerState</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I71910979841fd934153da109380a5078ba1a9741">I71910</a>)</li>
<li>A date input is now a display mode at the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>. Added support for switching between date picker and date input  modes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieeff707da21566b0b8d4fe365662ce6ae2a6acd1">Ieeff7</a>)</li>
<li>Added API for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RichTextTooltips</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I58ef33c950cdcb0461e0cf5f192fb730444d6fb4">I58ef3</a>)</li>
<li>Modal bottom sheet implementation for Material 3, including <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetDefaults</code>. Also introduces <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SheetState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberSheetState</code> which can be used for future sheet components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0853a6ec6d06166787701db1edb4a09b90dd563e">I0853a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/244189383">b/244189383</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Stablize the API <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showSnackbar</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I195c2c308e2597acf97dc90b5c0f3315b3556e90">I195c2</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261424370">b/261424370</a>)</li>
<li>Stablize the APIs for assist chip and suggestion chip (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibb67b1b2a21c8cb37213a22a76d49357b4097621">Ibb67b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261424370">b/261424370</a>)</li>
<li>Promotes <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListItem</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListItemDefaults</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListItemColors</code> API to non-experimental (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7e7faed87feb7ab15de0dbda181eda60d6a9cebc">I7e7fa</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261438882">b/261438882</a>)</li>
<li>Promoting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SliderPositions</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SliderDefaults.Thumb</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SliderDefaults.Track</code> to stable and adding non-experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSlider</code> APIs that contain custom thumbs and track. Also deprecating the previous <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeSlider</code> APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie5ea6c578fc9335e658305bdf2b64365eb4fab01">Ie5ea6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261566890">b/261566890</a>)</li>
<li>Made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.tooltipAnchor()</code> public, so devs can pass it to the anchor to indicate a tooltip should be displayed on long press. Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltipBox</code> API to no longer make <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TooltipState</code> nullable and now has a default. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie2fb71e5fdbe4266d075861f2eac972e1ba0de03">Ie2fb7</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ProgressIndicatorDefaults.circularTrackColor</code> has been marked <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Composable</code> for consistency. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id29cc370fda15a68076e546550582298a64f17b4">Id29cc</a>)</li>
<li>Restored property getter <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalMinimuTouchTargetEnforcement</code> and mark it as deprecated and redirect to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalMinimumInteractiveComponentEnforcement</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I60dd5ceb7c5703c8ba68f1b7d4a4a883b3f961a8">I60dd5</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>January 11, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha04</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha04</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/047e199bdcb8a5cd744cc7a2f986631bfb350ec7..adf1c279a86ab3886e1666c08e2c3efba783367b/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Initial <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> API for picking a single date via a calendar UI. This API is still undergoing changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I722b9884403da2d615167f6572a2da9256dbae2a">I722b9</a>)</li>
<li>Added support for plain tooltips via <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlainTooltipBox</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0cdfb8dc51bc3691b948184adc4fcb9cf61be107">I0cdfb</a>)</li>
<li>Search bar (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad1280bb7c3eaeac73116f73567bb6de07a81eb2">Iad128</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I458a8e1359896712a2a8aede43e0283977be4601">I458a8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/242889540">b/242889540</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IsContainer</code> semantics property on Surfaces. This property will be used in a later change that determines traversal order based on the semantic meaning of elements such as surfaces. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I63379fde102abbee7d5464c50b1c86a59e01e768">I63379</a>)</li>
<li>Mark navigation drawer related APIs as stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iab01ec21f7ef0de980ffc868f46b54966186e6ed">Iab01e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261439597">b/261439597</a>)</li>
<li>Added a track color parameter for circular progress indicators, and a stroke cap parameter for both circular and linear progress indicators. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie668cc47ce9ce3aa688ad3c3ed9e9e15fdbda5e9">Ie668c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/216325962">b/216325962</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222964817">b/222964817</a>)</li>
<li>More return type nullability of deprecated-hidden functions (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibf7b0ada56eb08983e6109d30fad5294f6b841f0">Ibf7b0</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.minimumInteractiveComponentSize</code>. It can be used to reserve at least 48.dp in size to disambiguate touch interactions if the element would measure smaller. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I33f58e4c11cf74668e97167b91dad26b64ac554b">I33f58</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/258495559">b/258495559</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental API for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> composable that has a content slot. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iec4a21dc5ad723f1a66527f3aea82a204fba4fd6">Iec4a2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Progress for progress indicators is now properly bounded to its expected range. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a7eb76931af76bac20dbd2879674a60c2899672">I8a7eb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/262262727">b/262262727</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Known Issue</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>When updating from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.foundation:1.4.0-alpha03</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.foundation:1.4.0-alpha04</code>, you might experience a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">java.lang.NoSuchFieldError</code> error. <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/265172081">Here</a> is where the issue was orginially reported. A fix has been submitted, and will be available on the next Compose update. As a work around, update your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3</code> libraries to the latest version(1.1.0-alpha04) or downgrade your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.foundation</code> to 1.4.0-alpha03.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>December 7, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha03</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha03</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a1e318590b217ecfce1b2de17eed2f18b6a680bb..047e199bdcb8a5cd744cc7a2f986631bfb350ec7/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie44e1304babf2007f6dc5894716ca92c2ef6d067">Ie44e1</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha02</h3>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha02</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b..a1e318590b217ecfce1b2de17eed2f18b6a680bb/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>October 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.1.0-alpha01</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.1.0-alpha01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b/compose/material3">Version 1.1.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixes to the top app bar when title is applied with a TextStyle and a Brush.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/If667ed1ddaa162e64279aff534f94250db4bf0b6">If667e</a>)</li>

<h4 id="window_size_class_2" data-text="Window Size Class" tabindex="-1">Window Size Class</h4>

<ul>
<li><p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">material3-window-size-class</code> is a new library that provides support for window size classes: a set of opinionated viewport breakpoints for you to design, develop, and test resizable application layouts against. You can use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">calculateWindowSizeClass</code> to retrieve a window size class instance, which you can use to determine how your UI should appear, such as showing a navigation rail instead of bottom navigation for larger window sizes. For more information and sample usage see the API reference <a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/windowsizeclass/package-summary">documentation</a> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowSizeClass</code>.</p></li>
<li><p>Please see this <a href="http://material.io/blog/material-3-compose-stable">blog post</a> for more details!</p></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta03" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta03</h3>

<p>September 21, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-beta03</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.0.0-beta03</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/520c85b133ddf020d8f9e0a9a2240ed75df1cdfa..bdce26bd7556b92d2d4d2af3de881dd8e2c51459/compose/material3">Version 1.0.0-beta03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenuDefaults</code> now exposes a padding value for menu items. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I34ee1c4b4f07261c704aad64d97565b3752ef650">I34ee1</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenuBoxScope</code> now has a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.menuAnchor()</code> modifier that should be passed to the text field for proper a11y behavior. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I27fa36b864d5b3c923b538b480dfcda76ab0e863">I27fa3</a>)</li>
<li>Adding two overloaded methods for the current Slider API to allow users to pass in a thumb or track to populate the slider. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I21c0022c3882f896f1d4ca855a24cec5d317f641">I21c00</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated dark theme color mapping for On Error Container to tone 90 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic561226d89432381ac900475cc0f677f7bc33ffe">Ic5612</a>)</li>
<li>Fix to allow setting a transparent background for small Material 3 top app bars. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I645e29cd35cefb6e8effb2e455b53c5ff777568a">I645e2</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/245575782">b/245575782</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta02</h3>

<p>September 7, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-beta02</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.0.0-beta02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d9910e143f859716fd850a1f0036147622d6089b..cce7b70f6a5ebf955cf748a73c18b63228b22c74/compose/material3">Version 1.0.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Default components insets introduced in m3 components in beta01 version no longer account for IME insets.</li>
<li>Material3 Scaffold component now has a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentWindowInsets</code> parameter, allowing to specify the amount of insets to handle for the content slot. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icf11a4169c801d2670d88066984328205f48bb4f">Icf11a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/243713323">b/243713323</a>)</li>
<li>Deprecates the experimental Material 3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SmallTopAppBar</code> function and introduces an equivalent <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TopAppBar</code> function. Please migrate your
usage to the new one. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I74404a64a5764ea02895358d2db5dc9bb18c5aba">I74404</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/226918634">b/226918634</a>)</li>
<li>Adds control over the top app bar fling and snap behaviors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I15c817b5c615d43c22d96ca8b5b539df03e68dfa">I15c81</a>)</li>
<li>Removes startIndent from Divider, moves color to last parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If7be24e6a8dc6b3386a4419b87ee275dd513d630">If7be2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Have Dialogs identify themselves to talkback users by announcing the word Dialog when they are displayed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I857ef62e308faf491c696679ebd570a2ac50f804">I857ef</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta01</h3>

<p>August 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-beta01</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.0.0-beta01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/bea814b246f89ff7244e3c6b0648f0b57e47897c..d9910e143f859716fd850a1f0036147622d6089b/compose/material3">Version 1.0.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Reference</strong></p>

<p>To see latest theming, component and other composables available check out the <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#overview">Compose Material 3 API reference overview</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated the Material 3 top app bar to snap into a fully collapsed to a fully extended state. Also, updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TopAppBarDefaults</code> behavior function to be Composables and provide default values for their top app bar state and animation spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I642b393470e6a29a8a02cb5589fea02f601be8ec">I642b3</a>)</li>
<li>Updated FAB component signatures to match surface API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3afaaa86e1ed658f4f7f8d2bb3cff19f8ff874be">I3afaa</a>)</li>
<li>Added insets Build-in support for Top app bars, drawers, navigation bar and rail. These components, when used separately or with Scaffold will automatically handle insets for developers. Note: This change doesn&#39;t add automatic handling of status bar icons and transparency of the status and navigation bars. Please, continue to do it manually to ensure the best edge-to-edge experience. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7e4e67bd1a84d62bd5ab1eddc7dbed8efdb471d1">I7e4e6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/183161866">b/183161866</a>)</li>
<li>Updated component defaults to reduce API surface for future flexibility and performance improvements. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I31820a25a7d9807634856b52fa7258c84a729ddc">I31820</a>)</li>
<li>Reordered chip and navigation drawer sheet parameters to maintain consistency within the API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I45d0bd7f072d80fca60c397cc294aa65bc80782d">I45d0b</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">startIndent</code> from Divider and moved color to be the last parameter.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If7be24e6a8dc6b3386a4419b87ee275dd513d630">If7be2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha16" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha16" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha16</h3>

<p>August 10, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha16</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.0.0-alpha16</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a7f0710ad21f556f0dde9bf7bdab6d2135170fd4..bea814b246f89ff7244e3c6b0648f0b57e47897c/compose/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha16 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Support specifying a custom width on a navigation drawer. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia7f10a73922f252481f6dbc448b6fa8fb21184e4">Ia7f10</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Reorder Tab and Leading icon tab parameters to maintain consistency within the API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie2637a746c3b0ad1ec937797f9c84ea0a492fae7">Ie2637</a>)</li>
