<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha10" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha10" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha10</h3>

<p>April 20, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha10</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3-window-size-class:1.0.0-alpha10</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/41a4e31408842caa2b58db5e4ee6ec708464425f/compose/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha10 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">material3-window-size-class</code> is a new library that provides support for window size classes: a set of opinionated viewport breakpoints for you to design, develop, and test resizable application layouts against. You can use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">calculateWindowSizeClass</code> to retrieve a window size class instance, which you can use to determine how your UI should appear, such as showing a navigation rail instead of bottom navigation for larger window sizes. For more information and sample usage see the API reference documentation for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowSizeClass</code>. For more information on window size class definitions, see the public guidance on supporting different screen sizes.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Adds default FAB elevation for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomAppBar</code>, removes trailing lambda from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomAppBar</code> with FAB. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I92c479d1978bc1d2a2e2d5f66d63afee870363fa">I92c47</a>)</li>
<li>Adds Material3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledIconButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledTonalIconButton</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedIconButton</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib2bda93643f833d04a989233cc3b1bc09bcdfa2d">Ib2bda</a>)</li>
<li>Updates Material 3 Snackbar API to accept color values for the optional action and dismiss-action. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibe4b49cdf157005f98eda5c1bb5a2e2c40668d63">Ibe4b4</a>)</li>
<li>Partial consumption (down OR position) has been deprecated in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code>.  You can use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">consume()</code> to consume the change completely.  You can use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isConsumed</code> to determine whether or not someone else has previously consumed the change.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange::copy()</code> now always makes a shallow copy. It means that copies of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code> will be consumed once one of the copies is consumed. If you want to create an unbound <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code>, use constructor instead. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie6be471e6ed2a843e38712922c2231fdfd26213a">Ie6be4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/225669674">b/225669674</a>)</li>
<li>Changes to the Cards API to receive the container and content colors via a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardColors</code> interface, and to support a disabled state for
clickable cards. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I927dfb2b7723e3d2f5c36de86c6ea9a78582c153">I927df</a>)</li>
<li>The parameter <code translate="no" dir="ltr">backgroundColor</code> has been renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">containerColor</code> in Material 3 text fields for improved consistency with other components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6fbd9b4114b8bbd699ed57a8ff1df73b8fd16c33">I6fbd9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updates to the standard <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> to align it with the Material3 spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I09eab8e771f182abcafaabf8679ce1374126181b">I09eab</a>)</li>
<li>Move the top bar height of material3 Scaffold into the padding passed to content, allowing the content to render underneath the top app bar. If the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PaddingValues</code> are ignored, then the content might be obscured by the top bar. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I83cbc17a8068a04ea8b18609f12bd9e103630229">I83cbc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/217776202">b/217776202</a>)</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>Fix at the Material3 Button to read its default text style value
from the MaterialTheme. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie62fcb0c42f3ec6940734f9c80989f0ee57bb99e">Ie62fc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>March 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha07</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9b2b3d8efd5f00bd4af903bbaa926f6a712d0bd8..33cb12e8aba043a05b40470a5ef3be1b35114fd5/compose/material3/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updates to Material 3 Surface API that brings back the
overloaded functions for clickable Surfaces, as well as adding a
function to support selectable and toggleable Surfaces. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4bf182d38d4c503cc5f16f5c966294d9f042930d">I4bf18</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyVerticalGrid</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyHorizontalGrid</code> are now stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I307c0ce412c7bc762e334e429013c0442bd22fde">I307c0</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyVerticalGrid/LazyHorizontalGrid</code> and all related apis were moved into .grid subpackage. Please update your imports from androidx.compose.foundation.lazy to androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.grid. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2d446e0bed6f27f0394b7dcab1152301e3404b0f">I2d446</a>)</li>
<li>Reverted previous change of relying solely on a View for
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowInsetsControllerCompat</code>, and again require a Window which is
required for managing some window flags. Deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ViewCompat.getWindowInsetsController</code> in favor of
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowCompat.getInsetsController</code> to ensure that the correct Window is
used (such as if the View is in a dialog). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I660aee32108b59516232b41e05b3f05ae2538554">I660ae</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/219572936">b/219572936</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyVerticalGrid</code> API to define cross axis sizes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I17723fdc6302a345dd643fb637e1644168a2a321">I17723</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updates to the Card API to follow changes at the Surface
API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3c8b9adfb1ece2e8861f8646620c47772270c25c">I3c8b9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>February 23, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha06</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/db2ecbef194afcddfaede22e1d884a8959a9277c..9b2b3d8efd5f00bd4af903bbaa926f6a712d0bd8/compose/material3/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationDrawerItem</code> is added that represents a single destination within the drawers (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic396fe99d1f26080a3e3a9d2ed505e72008c85aa">Ic396f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/218286829">b/218286829</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PermanentNavigationDrawer</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissibleNavigationDrawer</code> have been added as experimental APIs. Those are the drawers suitable well for large screen devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5f8abcd6137f0819ceccae0f8cacd2a44af5ad2e">I5f8ab</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/218286829">b/218286829</a>)</li>
<li>Adds Material 3 bottom app bar support (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic432a12f98ac1db62a8f38f1a02c937e8ed49172">Ic432a</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavigationDrawer</code> has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalNavigationDrawer</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1807d3c889c63efa7a569416daaed58d94a3b17a">I1807d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/218286829">b/218286829</a>)</li>
<li>Added Material 3 Slider class and tokens (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1ccee0420983203697b724abfda838a32895885b">I1ccee</a>)</li>
<li>Added Tab implementation, see the documentation for sample usage (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie0146154fa799787662992b74b6d39e49e669eb1">Ie0146</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue where the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TalkBack</code> screen reader linear navigation selected an empty top app bar title. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id46909e5999c82f0ec7ac702e9d3f7d78263973c">Id4690</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconSize</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatingActionButtonDefaults</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia71cf97eac903d9cf6b46195145c502122f478b0">Ia71cf</a>)</li>
<li>Bug fix for hidden <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> buttons when a long text is added with a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib2cc936b917bdb64c13fe92820c47482e0b1e200">Ib2cc9</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/216663029">b/216663029</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>February 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9dceceb54300ed028a7e8fc7a3454f270337ffde..db2ecbef194afcddfaede22e1d884a8959a9277c/compose/material3/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<p>Added Material Design 3 components</p>

<ul>
<li>Dropdown menu
<ul>
<li><a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#dropdownmenu">DropdownMenu</a>, <a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#dropdownmenuitem">DropdownMenuItem</a></li>
</ul></li>
<li><a href="https://m3.material.io/components/cards/overview">Cards</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#card">Card</a>, <a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#outlinedcard">OutlinedCard</a>, <a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#elevatedcard">ElevatedCard</a></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Surface</code> function that takes an onClick
callback. Clickable surfaces should be created with an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InteractionSource</code>
and a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.clickable()</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I211c691cf894c2c3cc6a4fbc60983a7bcb608cd4">I211c6</a>)</li>
<li>Added pressed and focused elevation support for FAB. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibb58423650a4765994c13db4743a666db9fcfe1c">Ibb584</a>)</li>
<li>Changed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Surface</code> API to receive an InteractionSource which allows
controlling its appearance in different states. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iafbc81a22ad4c1bf36d20ff34e081209f668a8e7">Iafbc8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added missing tertiary colors in dynamic color schemes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I456c4ebaa493451db1020cd30536f5dc1bea6e05">I456c4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/214588434">b/214588434</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>January 26, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f09f3e0f47cacc65a631115deac08ee8cc132ceb..9dceceb54300ed028a7e8fc7a3454f270337ffde/compose/material3/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NonRestartableComposable</code> to methods that are overloads
of existing methods without complex logic. This reduces compiler
generated memoization checks (equals) for all parameters which
are repeated in the inner function that is called. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I90490b1a28bada20840ab59e47245c00c6253d11">I90490</a>)</li>
<li>Added Material 3 divider. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ica5fc42b0d81b0443e99367a97628efc6053da90">Ica5fc</a>)</li>
<li>Mark the Checkbox and RadioButton with an experimental API
annotation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie44bbc92b214e8f55414ae46dcf6f9286c8531e8">Ie44bb</a>)</li>
<li>Added support for Material 3 progress indicators. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iff232ace50948f646ca8e7586343dba163628418">Iff232</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/205023841">b/205023841</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Update a disabled <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton&#39;s</code> container color to be transparent (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6b2483a1bc2d1964af3e7b61602a1161bbd92b90">I6b248</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/213339737">b/213339737</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>January 12, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/75784ce6dbac6faa5320e5898e9472f02ab8710c..f09f3e0f47cacc65a631115deac08ee8cc132ceb/compose/material3/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalIndication</code> to Material 3&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7ce4e5c232d16bd8991a2c3d26eb53c30edc9448">I7ce4e</a>)</li>
<li>Fix the corner radius that is applied for Checkboxes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38b03cda11bf28245a3af3d726ddd0bb9cbe8fa6">I38b03</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/175198975">b/175198975</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/202309440">b/202309440</a>)</li>

</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>December 1, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3:material3:1.0.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9aadd5bc6f9a252350ef0f107d0f3b14ea653028..75784ce6dbac6faa5320e5898e9472f02ab8710c/compose/material3/material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add support for checkbox and radiobutton.</li>
<li>Updated to be compatible with Kotlin <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.6.0</code></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Remove drawer from Material 3&#39;s scaffold. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I04f51fd532e4c4e3f43928a14407af5bae72514c">I04f51</a>)</li>
<li>Adds Material 3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code> support. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id55427028a18e4d72fea288413a2bc2eb8a148d6">Id5542</a>)</li>
<li>Adds Material 3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> support. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I20334d6768b9c335047006ddb7b8cdca4e11133b">I20334</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Reduce <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> ripple radius from 40dp to 20dp. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I68bbe3303f412d17dcc2b2836b30005acae9cc75">I68bbe</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/206674345">b/206674345</a>)</li>
<li>Port string fast path for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Text</code> changes from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">compose.material</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I30b0334952793d44f811e8df63096811b0b164ee">I30b03</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed but that hardcoded button to always be enabled. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iea83268475294e78cb91b5da802d11ab4a7a6f3a">Iea832</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/205335456">b/205335456</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha01</h3>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<p>Material Design 3 theming and Material You dynamic color</p>
